[2013/03/07 14:33:59]:INSERT INTO TMP_RUFC1 SELECT @CONT:= IF(DEBIT LIKE CONCAT("","%"),DEBIT,IF(CREDIT LIKE CONCAT("","%"),CREDIT,"")) CONTFC, IFNULL(LEFT(DEND,3),"Doc") TIPD, NRDI, DATAI, DATASC, NRDE, DATAE, NRNIR, NRN, GEST, EXPLICN, CODFUR, IF(NOT (DEBIT = @CONT), DEBIT, CREDIT) CONT_COR, SUM(IF(DEBIT = @CONT, SUMA, 0)) DEBIT, SUM(IF(CREDIT = @CONT, SUMA, 0)) CREDIT FROM TMP_FISA1 LEFT JOIN TIPD ON (TIPDI = TIPD) GROUP BY CODFUR, NRDI, DATAI, NRDE, DATAE, NRNIR, DATANIR, CONTFC, NRN ORDER BY CONTFC, CONCAT(MID(DATAI,5,4), MID(DATAI,3,2),MID(DATAI,1,2)), NRDI,  CONT_COR

[2013/03/07 16:16:24]:INSERT INTO TMP_RUFC1 SELECT @CONT:= IF(DEBIT LIKE CONCAT("","%"),DEBIT,IF(CREDIT LIKE CONCAT("","%"),CREDIT,"")) CONTFC, IFNULL(LEFT(DEND,3),"Doc") TIPD, NRDI, DATAI, DATASC, NRDE, DATAE, NRNIR, NRN, GEST, EXPLICN, CODFUR, IF(NOT (DEBIT = @CONT), DEBIT, CREDIT) CONT_COR, SUM(IF(DEBIT = @CONT, SUMA, 0)) DEBIT, SUM(IF(CREDIT = @CONT, SUMA, 0)) CREDIT FROM TMP_FISA1 LEFT JOIN TIPD ON (TIPDI = TIPD) GROUP BY CODFUR, NRDI, DATAI, NRDE, DATAE, NRNIR, DATANIR, CONTFC, NRN ORDER BY CONTFC, CONCAT(MID(DATAI,5,4), MID(DATAI,3,2),MID(DATAI,1,2)), NRDI,  CONT_COR

[2013/03/08 10:17:22]:INSERT INTO TMP_RUFC1 SELECT @CONT := IF(URM = "D", DEBIT, CREDIT) CONTFC, IFNULL(LEFT(DEND,3),"Doc") TIPD, NRDI, DATAI, DATASC, NRDE, DATAE, NRNIR, NRN, GEST, EXPLICN, CODFUR, IF(NOT (DEBIT = @CONT), DEBIT, CREDIT) CONT_COR, SUM(IF(DEBIT = @CONT, SUMA, 0)) DEBIT, SUM(IF(CREDIT = @CONT, SUMA, 0)) CREDIT FROM TMP_FISA1 LEFT JOIN TIPD ON (TIPDI = TIPD) WHERE URM <> "" GROUP BY CODFUR, NRDI, DATAI, NRDE, DATAE, NRNIR, DATANIR, CONTFC, NRN ORDER BY CONTFC, CONCAT(MID(DATAI,5,4), MID(DATAI,3,2),MID(DATAI,1,2)), NRDI,  CONT_COR
